userland@localhost:~$ # Check HTTP status for each subdomain and save to alive.txt
while read host; do                                               status=$(curl -k -o /dev/null -s -w "%{http_code}" https://$host)
echo "$host $status"                                          done < final_subs.txt > alive.txt
